    12	        public static DatabaseType ToDatabaseType(this string providerAlias, bool isDacpac)
    13	        {
    14	            if (!GetKnownProviders().TryGetValue(providerAlias, out var provider))
    15	            {
    16	                return DatabaseType.Undefined;
    17	            }
    18	
    19	            switch (provider)
    20	            {
    21	                case "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer":
    22	                    if (isDacpac)
    23	                    {
    24	                        return DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac;
    25	                    }
    26	
    27	                    return DatabaseType.SQLServer;
    28	
    29	                case "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Sqlite":
    30	                    return DatabaseType.SQLite;
    31	
    32	                case "Npgsql.EntityFrameworkCore.PostgreSQL":
    33	                    return DatabaseType.Npgsql;
    34	
    35	                case "Pomelo.EntityFrameworkCore.MySql":
    36	                    return DatabaseType.Mysql;
    37	
    38	                case "Oracle.EntityFrameworkCore":
    39	                    return DatabaseType.Oracle;
    40	
    41	                case "FirebirdSql.EntityFrameworkCore.Firebird":
    42	                    return DatabaseType.Firebird;
    43	
    44	                case "EFCore.Snowflake":
    45	                    return DatabaseType.Snowflake;
    46	
    47	                default:
    48	                    return DatabaseType.Undefined;
    49	            }
    50	        }
    51	
    52	        public static string ToDatabaseShortName(this DatabaseType databaseType)
    53	        {
    54	            switch (databaseType)
    55	            {
    56	                case DatabaseType.Undefined:
    57	                    return "Undefined";
    58	                case DatabaseType.SQLServer:
    59	                    return "mssql";
    60	                case DatabaseType.SQLite:
    61	                    return "sqlite";
    62	                case DatabaseType.Npgsql:
    63	                    return "npgsql";
    64	                case DatabaseType.Mysql:
    65	                    return "mysql";
    66	                case DatabaseType.Oracle:
    67	                    return "oracle";
    68	                case DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac:
    69	                    return "mssql";
    70	                case DatabaseType.Firebird:
    71	                    return "firebird";
    72	                case DatabaseType.Snowflake:
    73	                    return "snowflake";
    74	                default:
    75	                    return "Undefined";
    76	            }
    77	        }

    90	        public static string CreateReadme(ReverseEngineerCommandOptions commandOptions, CodeGenerationMode codeGenerationMode, string redactedConnectionString)
    91	        {
    92	            if (commandOptions == null)
    93	            {
    94	                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(commandOptions));
    95	            }
    96	
    97	            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(redactedConnectionString))
    98	            {
    99	                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(redactedConnectionString));
   100	            }
   101	
   102	            var packages = GetNeededPackages(
   103	                commandOptions.DatabaseType,
   104	                commandOptions.UseSpatial,
   105	                commandOptions.UseNodaTime,
   106	                commandOptions.UseDateOnlyTimeOnly,
   107	                commandOptions.UseHierarchyId,
   108	                commandOptions.UseMultipleSprocResultSets,
   109	                commandOptions.Tables?.Exists(t => t.ObjectType == ObjectType.Procedure) ?? false,
   110	                codeGenerationMode);
   111	
   112	            var readmeName = "efcpt-readme.md";
   113	
   114	            var template = File.ReadAllText(Path.Combine(Path.GetDirectoryName(Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().Location), readmeName), Encoding.UTF8);
   115	
   116	            var finalText = GetReadMeText(commandOptions, template, packages, redactedConnectionString);
   117	
   118	            var readmePath = Path.Combine(commandOptions.ProjectPath, readmeName);
   119	
   120	            File.WriteAllText(readmePath, finalText, Encoding.UTF8);
   121	
   122	            return readmePath;
   123	        }

   459	        private static string GetReadMeText(ReverseEngineerCommandOptions options, string content, List<NuGetPackage> packages, string redactedConnectionString)
   460	        {
   461	            var extraPackages = packages.Where(p => !p.IsMainProviderPackage && p.UseMethodName != null)
   462	                .Select(p => $"Use{p.UseMethodName}()").ToList();
   463	
   464	            var useText = string.Empty;
   465	
   466	            if (extraPackages.Count > 0)
   467	            {
   468	                useText = "," + Environment.NewLine + "           x => x." + string.Join(".", extraPackages);
   469	            }
   470	
   471	            var packageText = new StringBuilder();
   472	
   473	            foreach (var package in packages)
   474	            {
   475	                packageText.AppendLine($"  <PackageReference Include=\"{package.PackageId}\" Version=\"{package.Version}\" />");
   476	            }
   477	
   478	            var mainPackage = packages.Find(p => p.IsMainProviderPackage);
   479	
   480	            return content.Replace("[ProviderName]", mainPackage?.UseMethodName ?? string.Empty)
   481	                .Replace("[ConnectionString]", redactedConnectionString.Replace(@"\", @"\\"))
   482	                .Replace("[UseList]", useText)
   483	                .Replace("[PackageList]", packageText.ToString())
   484	                .Replace("[ContextName]", options.ContextClassName);
   485	        }
   486	
   487	        private static Dictionary<string, string> GetKnownProviders()
   488	        {
   489	            var result = new Dictionary<string, string>();
   490	
   491	            foreach (var provider in GetProvidersWithAliases())
   492	            {
   493	                result.Add(provider.Key, provider.Key);
   494	
   495	                foreach (var item in provider.Value)
   496	                {
   497	                    result.Add(item, provider.Key);
   498	                }
   499	            }
   500	
   501	            return result;
   502	        }
   503	
   504	        private static Dictionary<string, List<string>> GetProvidersWithAliases()
   505	        {
   506	            return new Dictionary<string, List<string>>
   507	            {
   508	                {
   509	                    "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer",
   510	                    new List<string> { "mssql", "sqlserver" }
   511	                },
   512	                {
   513	                    "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Sqlite",
   514	                    new List<string> { "sqlite" }
   515	                },
   516	                {
   517	                    "Npgsql.EntityFrameworkCore.PostgreSQL",
   518	                    new List<string> { "postgres", "postgresql" }
   519	                },
   520	                {
   521	                    "Pomelo.EntityFrameworkCore.MySql",
   522	                    new List<string> { "mysql" }
   523	                },
   524	                {
   525	                    "Oracle.EntityFrameworkCore",
   526	                    new List<string> { "oracle" }
   527	                },
   528	                {
   529	                    "FirebirdSql.EntityFrameworkCore.Firebird",
   530	                    new List<string> { "firebird" }
   531	                },
   532	                {
   533	                    "EFCore.Snowflake",
   534	                    new List<string> { "snowflake" }
   535	                },
   536	            };
   537	        }

     1	using System;

    12	using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Design.Internal;

    28	using Pomelo.EntityFrameworkCore.MySql.Design.Internal;

    34	namespace RevEng.Core
    35	{
    36	    public static class ServiceProviderBuilder
    37	    {
    38	        public static IServiceCollection AddEfpt(this IServiceCollection serviceCollection, ReverseEngineerCommandOptions options, List<string> errors, List<string> warnings, List<string> info)
    39	        {
    40	            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(options);
    41	            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(serviceCollection);
    42	            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(warnings);
    43	            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(errors);
    44	            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(info);
    45	
    46	            var reporter = new OperationReporter(
    47	                new OperationReportHandler(
    48	                    errors.Add,
    49	                    warnings.Add,
    50	                    info.Add,
    51	                    info.Add));
    52	
    53	            serviceCollection
    54	                .AddEntityFrameworkDesignTimeServices()
    55	                .AddSingleton<IOperationReporter, OperationReporter>(provider =>
    56	                    reporter)
    57	                .AddSingleton<IScaffoldingModelFactory>(provider =>
    58	                    new ColumnRemovingScaffoldingModelFactory(
    59	                        provider.GetService<IOperationReporter>(),
    60	                        provider.GetService<ICandidateNamingService>(),
    61	                        provider.GetService<IPluralizer>(),
    62	                        provider.GetService<ICSharpUtilities>(),
    63	                        provider.GetService<IScaffoldingTypeMapper>(),
    64	                        provider.GetService<LoggingDefinitions>(),
    65	                        provider.GetService<IModelRuntimeInitializer>(),
    66	                        options.Tables,
    67	                        options.DatabaseType,
    68	                        options.UseManyToManyEntity));
    69	
    70	            if (options.CustomReplacers != null || options.UsePrefixNavigationNaming)
    71	            {
    72	                serviceCollection.AddSingleton<ICandidateNamingService>(provider => new ReplacingCandidateNamingService(options.UsePrefixNavigationNaming, options.CustomReplacers, options.PreserveCasingWithRegex));
    73	            }
    74	
    75	            if (options.UseHandleBars)
    76	            {
    77	                serviceCollection.AddHandlebarsScaffolding(hbOptions =>
    78	                {
    79	                    hbOptions.ReverseEngineerOptions = Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Design.ReverseEngineerOptions.DbContextAndEntities;
    80	                    hbOptions.LanguageOptions = (LanguageOptions)options.SelectedHandlebarsLanguage;
    81	                });
    82	                serviceCollection.AddSingleton<ITemplateFileService>(provider
    83	                    => new CustomTemplateFileService(options.OptionsPath));
    84	            }
    85	
    86	            if (options.UseInflector || options.UseLegacyPluralizer)
    87	            {
    88	                if (options.UseLegacyPluralizer)
    89	                {
    90	                    serviceCollection.AddSingleton<IPluralizer, LegacyPluralizer>();
    91	                }
    92	                else
    93	                {
    94	                    if (options.IrregularWords != null && options.IrregularWords.Count > 0)
    95	                    {
    96	                        options.IrregularWords.ForEach(w => Vocabularies.Default.AddIrregular(w.Singular, w.Plural, w.MatchEnding));
    97	                    }
    98	
    99	                    if (options.UncountableWords != null && options.UncountableWords.Count > 0)
   100	                    {
   101	                        options.UncountableWords.ForEach(w => Vocabularies.Default.AddUncountable(w));
   102	                    }
   103	
   104	                    if (options.PluralRules != null && options.PluralRules.Count > 0)
   105	                    {
   106	                        options.PluralRules.ForEach(w => Vocabularies.Default.AddPlural(w.Rule, w.Replacement));
   107	                    }
   108	
   109	                    if (options.SingularRules != null && options.SingularRules.Count > 0)
   110	                    {
   111	                        options.SingularRules.ForEach(w => Vocabularies.Default.AddSingular(w.Rule, w.Replacement));
   112	                    }
   113	
   114	                    serviceCollection.AddSingleton<IPluralizer, HumanizerPluralizer>();
   115	                }
   116	            }
   117	
   118	            serviceCollection.AddNotImplementedDesignTimeServices();
   119	
   120	            // Add database provider services
   121	            switch (options.DatabaseType)
   122	            {
   123	                case DatabaseType.SQLServer:
   124	                case DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac:
   125	                    AddSqlServerProviderServices(serviceCollection, options);
   126	                    break;
   127	
   128	                case DatabaseType.Npgsql:
   129	                    AddPostgresProviderServices(serviceCollection, options);
   130	                    break;
   131	
   132	                case DatabaseType.Oracle:
   133	                    var oracleProvider = new OracleDesignTimeServices();
   134	                    oracleProvider.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   135	
   136	#if CORE100
   137	                    if (options.UseSpatial)
   138	                    {
   139	                        var spatial = new OracleNetTopologySuiteDesignTimeServices();
   140	                        spatial.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   141	                    }
   142	#endif
   143	                    break;
   144	
   145	#if !CORE100
   146	                case DatabaseType.Mysql:
   147	                    var mysqlProvider = new MySqlDesignTimeServices();
   148	                    mysqlProvider.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   149	
   150	                    if (options.UseSpatial)
   151	                    {
   152	                        var spatial = new MySqlNetTopologySuiteDesignTimeServices();
   153	                        spatial.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   154	                    }
   155	
   156	                    break;
   157	#endif
   158	
   159	                case DatabaseType.Firebird:
   160	                    var firebirdProvider = new FbDesignTimeServices();
   161	                    firebirdProvider.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   162	                    break;
   163	#if !CORE100
   164	                case DatabaseType.Snowflake:
   165	                    var snowflakeProvider = new SnowflakeDesignTimeServices();
   166	                    snowflakeProvider.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   167	                    break;
   168	#endif
   169	
   170	                case DatabaseType.SQLite:
   171	                    var sqliteProvider = new SqliteDesignTimeServices();
   172	                    sqliteProvider.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   173	
   174	#if !CORE100
   175	                    if (options.UseNodaTime)
   176	                    {
   177	                        var nodaTime = new SqliteNodaTimeDesignTimeServices();
   178	                        nodaTime.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   179	                    }
   180	#endif
   181	                    break;
   182	
   183	                default:
   184	                    throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(options), $"unsupported database type: {options.DatabaseType}");
   185	            }
   186	
   187	            serviceCollection.AddSingleton<IReverseEngineerScaffolder, ReverseEngineerScaffolder>();
   188	
   189	            return serviceCollection;
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        private static void AddPostgresProviderServices(IServiceCollection serviceCollection, ReverseEngineerCommandOptions options)
   193	        {
   194	            var npgsqlProvider = new NpgsqlDesignTimeServices();
   195	            npgsqlProvider.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   196	
   197	            serviceCollection.AddPostgresStoredProcedureDesignTimeServices();
   198	
   199	            if (options.UseNodaTime)
   200	            {
   201	                var nodaTime = new NpgsqlNodaTimeDesignTimeServices();
   202	                nodaTime.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   203	            }
   204	
   205	            if (options.UseSpatial)
   206	            {
   207	                var spatial = new NpgsqlNetTopologySuiteDesignTimeServices();
   208	                spatial.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   209	            }
   210	        }
   211	
   212	        private static void AddSqlServerProviderServices(IServiceCollection serviceCollection, ReverseEngineerCommandOptions options)
   213	        {
   214	            var provider = new SqlServerDesignTimeServices();
   215	            provider.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   216	
   217	#if CORE100
   218	            serviceCollection.AddSingleton(new SqlServerSingletonOptions());
   219	#endif
   220	
   221	            if (options.DatabaseType == DatabaseType.SQLServer)
   222	            {
   223	                serviceCollection.AddSingleton(options);
   224	                serviceCollection.AddSingleton<IDatabaseModelFactory, PatchedSqlServerDatabaseModelFactory>();
   225	                serviceCollection.AddSqlServerStoredProcedureDesignTimeServices();
   226	                serviceCollection.AddSqlServerFunctionDesignTimeServices();
   227	            }
   228	
   229	            if (options.DatabaseType == DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac)
   230	            {
   231	                var excludedIndexes = options.Tables?.Select(t => new { t.Name, t.ExcludedIndexes });
   232	
   233	                serviceCollection.AddSingleton<IDatabaseModelFactory, SqlServerDacpacDatabaseModelFactory>(
   234	                   serviceProvider => new SqlServerDacpacDatabaseModelFactory(
   235	                       new SqlServerDacpacDatabaseModelFactoryOptions
   236	                       {
   237	                           MergeDacpacs = options.MergeDacpacs,
   238	                           ExcludedIndexes = excludedIndexes?.ToDictionary(t => t.Name, t => t.ExcludedIndexes),
   239	                       },
   240	                       serviceProvider.GetService<IRelationalTypeMappingSource>()));
   241	
   242	                serviceCollection.AddSqlServerDacpacStoredProcedureDesignTimeServices(new SqlServerDacpacDatabaseModelFactoryOptions
   243	                {
   244	                    MergeDacpacs = options.MergeDacpacs,
   245	                });
   246	
   247	                serviceCollection.AddSqlServerDacpacFunctionDesignTimeServices(new SqlServerDacpacDatabaseModelFactoryOptions
   248	                {
   249	                    MergeDacpacs = options.MergeDacpacs,
   250	                });
   251	            }
   252	
   253	            if (options.UseSpatial)
   254	            {
   255	                var spatial = new SqlServerNetTopologySuiteDesignTimeServices();
   256	                spatial.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   257	            }
   258	
   259	            if (options.UseHierarchyId)
   260	            {
   261	                var hierachyId = new SqlServerHierarchyIdDesignTimeServices();
   262	                hierachyId.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   263	            }
   264	
   265	            if (options.UseNodaTime)
   266	            {
   267	                var nodaTime = new SqlServerNodaTimeDesignTimeServices();
   268	                nodaTime.ConfigureDesignTimeServices(serviceCollection);
   269	            }
   270	
   271	#if !CORE100
   272	            serviceCollection.AddSingleton<IRelationalTypeMappingSource, SqlServerTypeMappingSource>(
   273	                provider => new SqlServerTypeMappingSource(
   274	                    provider.GetService<TypeMappingSourceDependencies>(),
   275	                    provider.GetService<RelationalTypeMappingSourceDependencies>(),
   276	                    options.UseDateOnlyTimeOnly));
   277	#else
   278	            serviceCollection.AddSingleton<IRelationalTypeMappingSource, SqlServerTypeMappingSource>(
   279	                provider => new SqlServerTypeMappingSource(
   280	                    provider.GetService<TypeMappingSourceDependencies>(),
   281	                    provider.GetService<RelationalTypeMappingSourceDependencies>(),
   282	                    provider.GetService<SqlServerSingletonOptions>(),
   283	                    options.UseDateOnlyTimeOnly));
   284	#endif
   285	        }
   286	    }
   287	}

    12	        public static DatabaseType ToDatabaseType(this string providerAlias, bool isDacpac)
    13	        {
    14	            if (!GetKnownProviders().TryGetValue(providerAlias, out var provider))
    15	            {
    16	                return DatabaseType.Undefined;
    17	            }
    18	
    19	            switch (provider)
    20	            {
    21	                case "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer":
    22	                    if (isDacpac)
    23	                    {
    24	                        return DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac;
    25	                    }
    26	
    27	                    return DatabaseType.SQLServer;
    28	
    29	                case "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Sqlite":
    30	                    return DatabaseType.SQLite;
    31	
    32	                case "Npgsql.EntityFrameworkCore.PostgreSQL":
    33	                    return DatabaseType.Npgsql;
    34	
    35	                case "Pomelo.EntityFrameworkCore.MySql":
    36	                    return DatabaseType.Mysql;
    37	
    38	                case "Oracle.EntityFrameworkCore":
    39	                    return DatabaseType.Oracle;
    40	
    41	                case "FirebirdSql.EntityFrameworkCore.Firebird":
    42	                    return DatabaseType.Firebird;
    43	
    44	                case "EFCore.Snowflake":
    45	                    return DatabaseType.Snowflake;
    46	
    47	                default:
    48	                    return DatabaseType.Undefined;
    49	            }
    50	        }
    51	
    52	        public static string ToDatabaseShortName(this DatabaseType databaseType)
    53	        {
    54	            switch (databaseType)
    55	            {
    56	                case DatabaseType.Undefined:
    57	                    return "Undefined";
    58	                case DatabaseType.SQLServer:
    59	                    return "mssql";
    60	                case DatabaseType.SQLite:
    61	                    return "sqlite";
    62	                case DatabaseType.Npgsql:
    63	                    return "npgsql";
    64	                case DatabaseType.Mysql:
    65	                    return "mysql";
    66	                case DatabaseType.Oracle:
    67	                    return "oracle";
    68	                case DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac:
    69	                    return "mssql";
    70	                case DatabaseType.Firebird:
    71	                    return "firebird";
    72	                case DatabaseType.Snowflake:
    73	                    return "snowflake";
    74	                default:
    75	                    return "Undefined";
    76	            }
    77	        }

    89	
    90	        public static string CreateReadme(ReverseEngineerCommandOptions commandOptions, CodeGenerationMode codeGenerationMode, string redactedConnectionString)
    91	        {
    92	            if (commandOptions == null)
    93	            {
    94	                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(commandOptions));
    95	            }
    96	
    97	            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(redactedConnectionString))
    98	            {
    99	                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(redactedConnectionString));
   100	            }
   101	
   102	            var packages = GetNeededPackages(
   103	                commandOptions.DatabaseType,
   104	                commandOptions.UseSpatial,
   105	                commandOptions.UseNodaTime,
   106	                commandOptions.UseDateOnlyTimeOnly,
   107	                commandOptions.UseHierarchyId,
   108	                commandOptions.UseMultipleSprocResultSets,
   109	                commandOptions.Tables?.Exists(t => t.ObjectType == ObjectType.Procedure) ?? false,
   110	                codeGenerationMode);
   111	
   112	            var readmeName = "efcpt-readme.md";
   113	
   114	            var template = File.ReadAllText(Path.Combine(Path.GetDirectoryName(Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().Location), readmeName), Encoding.UTF8);
   115	
   116	            var finalText = GetReadMeText(commandOptions, template, packages, redactedConnectionString);
   117	
   118	            var readmePath = Path.Combine(commandOptions.ProjectPath, readmeName);
   119	
   120	            File.WriteAllText(readmePath, finalText, Encoding.UTF8);
   121	
   122	            return readmePath;
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        public static List<NuGetPackage> GetNeededPackages(DatabaseType databaseType, bool useSpatial, bool useNodaTime, bool useDateOnlyTimeOnly, bool useHierarchyId, bool discoverMultipleResultSets, bool hasProcedures, CodeGenerationMode codeGenerationMode)
   126	        {
   127	            // Update versions here when adding provider and other updates
   128	            var packages = new List<NuGetPackage>();
   129	
   130	            if (databaseType == DatabaseType.SQLServer || databaseType == DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac)
   131	            {
   132	                var pkgVersion = string.Empty;
   133	                switch (codeGenerationMode)
   134	                {
   135	                    case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore8:
   136	                        pkgVersion = "8.0.26";
   137	                        break;
   138	                    case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore9:
   139	                        pkgVersion = "9.0.15";
   140	                        break;
   141	                    case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore10:
   142	                        pkgVersion = "10.0.6";
   143	                        break;
   144	
   145	                    default:
   146	                        throw new NotImplementedException();
   147	                }
   148	
   149	                packages.Add(new NuGetPackage
   150	                {
   151	                    PackageId = "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer",
   152	                    Version = pkgVersion,
   153	                    DatabaseTypes = new List<DatabaseType> { DatabaseType.SQLServer, DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac },
   154	                    IsMainProviderPackage = true,
   155	                    UseMethodName = "SqlServer",
   156	                });
   157	
   158	                if (useSpatial)
   159	                {
   160	                    packages.Add(new NuGetPackage
   161	                    {
   162	                        PackageId = "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer.NetTopologySuite",
   163	                        Version = pkgVersion,
   164	                        DatabaseTypes = new List<DatabaseType> { DatabaseType.SQLServer, DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac },
   165	                        IsMainProviderPackage = false,
   166	                        UseMethodName = "NetTopologySuite",
   167	                    });
   168	                }
   169	
   170	                if (useHierarchyId)
   171	                {
   172	                    packages.Add(new NuGetPackage
   173	                    {
   174	                        PackageId = "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer.HierarchyId",
   175	                        Version = pkgVersion,
   176	                        DatabaseTypes = new List<DatabaseType> { DatabaseType.SQLServer, DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac },
   177	                        IsMainProviderPackage = false,
   178	                        UseMethodName = "HierarchyId",
   179	                    });
   180	                }
   181	
   182	                if (useNodaTime)
   183	                {
   184	                    switch (codeGenerationMode)
   185	                    {
   186	                        case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore8:
   187	                            pkgVersion = "8.0.1";
   188	                            break;
   189	
   190	                        case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore9:
   191	                            pkgVersion = "9.1.1";
   192	                            break;
   193	
   194	                        case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore10:
   195	                            pkgVersion = "10.0.0";
   196	                            break;
   197	
   198	                        default: throw new NotImplementedException();
   199	                    }
   200	
   201	                    packages.Add(new NuGetPackage
   202	                    {
   203	                        PackageId = "SimplerSoftware.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer.NodaTime",
   204	                        Version = pkgVersion,
   205	                        DatabaseTypes = new List<DatabaseType> { DatabaseType.SQLServer, DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac },
   206	                        IsMainProviderPackage = false,
   207	                        UseMethodName = "NodaTime",
   208	                    });
   209	                }
   210	
   211	                if (hasProcedures && discoverMultipleResultSets)
   212	                {
   213	                    packages.Add(new NuGetPackage
   214	                    {
   215	                        PackageId = "Dapper",
   216	                        Version = "2.1.66",
   217	                        DatabaseTypes = new List<DatabaseType> { DatabaseType.SQLServer, DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac },
   218	                        IsMainProviderPackage = false,
   219	                        UseMethodName = null,
   220	                    });
   221	                }
   222	            }
   223

   225	            {

   227	                switch (codeGenerationMode)
   228	                {
   229	                    case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore8:

   231	                        break;

   242	                }
   243	
   244	                packages.Add(new NuGetPackage
   245	                {

   247	                    Version = pkgVersion,
   248	                    DatabaseTypes = new List<DatabaseType> { databaseType },
   249	                    IsMainProviderPackage = true,

   251	                });
   252	
   253	                if (useNodaTime)

open my $out, '>', 'src/Core/RevEng.Core.80/ServiceProviderBuilder.cs' or die $!;
print $out $content;
close $out;
print "Done\n";

+using System;
+using System.Collections.Generic;
+using System.IO;
+using System.Linq;
+using System.Reflection;
+using System.Text;
+
+namespace RevEng.Common
+{
+    public static class Providers
+    {
+        public static DatabaseType ToDatabaseType(this string providerAlias, bool isDacpac)
+        {
+            if (!GetKnownProviders().TryGetValue(providerAlias, out var provider))
+            {
+                return DatabaseType.Undefined;
+            }
+
+            switch (provider)
+            {
+                case "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer":
+                    if (isDacpac)
+                    {
+                        return DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac;
+                    }
+
+                    return DatabaseType.SQLServer;
+
+                case "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Sqlite":
+                    return DatabaseType.SQLite;
+
+                case "Npgsql.EntityFrameworkCore.PostgreSQL":
+                    return DatabaseType.Npgsql;
+
+                case "Pomelo.EntityFrameworkCore.MySql":
+                    return DatabaseType.Mysql;
+
+                case "Oracle.EntityFrameworkCore":
+                    return DatabaseType.Oracle;
+
+                case "FirebirdSql.EntityFrameworkCore.Firebird":
+                    return DatabaseType.Firebird;
+
+                case "EFCore.Snowflake":
+                    return DatabaseType.Snowflake;
+
+                default:
+                    return DatabaseType.Undefined;
+            }
+        }
+
+        public static string ToDatabaseShortName(this DatabaseType databaseType)
+        {
+            switch (databaseType)
+            {
+                case DatabaseType.Undefined:
+                    return "Undefined";
+                case DatabaseType.SQLServer:
+                    return "mssql";
+                case DatabaseType.SQLite:
+                    return "sqlite";
+                case DatabaseType.Npgsql:
+                    return "npgsql";
+                case DatabaseType.Mysql:
+                    return "mysql";
+                case DatabaseType.Oracle:
+                    return "oracle";
+                case DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac:
+                    return "mssql";
+                case DatabaseType.Firebird:
+                    return "firebird";
+                case DatabaseType.Snowflake:
+                    return "snowflake";
+                default:
+                    return "Undefined";
+            }
+        }

+        public static HashSet<DatabaseType> GetDabProviders()
+            {
+            return new HashSet<DatabaseType>
+            {
+                DatabaseType.SQLServer,
+                DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac,
+                DatabaseType.Npgsql,
+                DatabaseType.Mysql,
+            };

+
+        public static string CreateReadme(ReverseEngineerCommandOptions commandOptions, CodeGenerationMode codeGenerationMode, string redactedConnectionString)
+        {
+            if (commandOptions == null)
+            {
+                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(commandOptions));
+            }
+
+            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(redactedConnectionString))
+            {
+                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(redactedConnectionString));
+            }
+
+            var packages = GetNeededPackages(
+                commandOptions.DatabaseType,
+                commandOptions.UseSpatial,
+                commandOptions.UseNodaTime,
+                commandOptions.UseDateOnlyTimeOnly,
+                commandOptions.UseHierarchyId,
+                commandOptions.UseMultipleSprocResultSets,
+                commandOptions.Tables?.Exists(t => t.ObjectType == ObjectType.Procedure) ?? false,
+                codeGenerationMode);
+
+            var readmeName = "efcpt-readme.md";
+
+            var template = File.ReadAllText(Path.Combine(Path.GetDirectoryName(Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().Location), readmeName), Encoding.UTF8);
+
+            var finalText = GetReadMeText(commandOptions, template, packages, redactedConnectionString);
+
+            var readmePath = Path.Combine(commandOptions.ProjectPath, readmeName);
+
+            File.WriteAllText(readmePath, finalText, Encoding.UTF8);
+
+            return readmePath;
+        }

+        public static List<NuGetPackage> GetNeededPackages(DatabaseType databaseType, bool useSpatial, bool useNodaTime, bool useDateOnlyTimeOnly, bool useHierarchyId, bool discoverMultipleResultSets, bool hasProcedures, CodeGenerationMode codeGenerationMode)
+        {
+            // Update versions here when adding provider and other updates
+            var packages = new List<NuGetPackage>();
+
+            if (databaseType == DatabaseType.SQLServer || databaseType == DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac)
+            {
+                var pkgVersion = string.Empty;
+                switch (codeGenerationMode)
+                {
+                    case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore8:
+                        pkgVersion = "8.0.26";
+                        break;
+                    case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore9:
+                        pkgVersion = "9.0.15";
+                        break;
+                    case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore10:
+                        pkgVersion = "10.0.6";
+                        break;
+
+                    default:
+                        throw new NotImplementedException();
+                }
+
+                packages.Add(new NuGetPackage
+                {
+                    PackageId = "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer",
+                    Version = pkgVersion,
+                    DatabaseTypes = new List<DatabaseType> { DatabaseType.SQLServer, DatabaseType.SQLServerDacpac },
+                    IsMainProviderPackage = true,
+                    UseMethodName = "SqlServer",
+                });
+
+                if (useSpatial)
+                {

+                    {
+                        PackageId = "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer.NetTopologySuite",

+                        UseMethodName = "HierarchyId",

+                if (useNodaTime)
+                {

+                        case CodeGenerationMode.EFCore9:

+                        IsMainProviderPackage = false,

+        private static string GetReadMeText(ReverseEngineerCommandOptions options, string content, List<NuGetPackage> packages, string redactedConnectionString)
+        {
+            var extraPackages = packages.Where(p => !p.IsMainProviderPackage && p.UseMethodName != null)
+                .Select(p => $"Use{p.UseMethodName}()").ToList();
+
+            var useText = string.Empty;
+
+            if (extraPackages.Count > 0)
+            {
+                useText = "," + Environment.NewLine + "           x => x." + string.Join(".", extraPackages);
+            }
+
+            var packageText = new StringBuilder();
+
+            foreach (var package in packages)
+            {
+                packageText.AppendLine($"  <PackageReference Include=\"{package.PackageId}\" Version=\"{package.Version}\" />");
+            }
+
+            var mainPackage = packages.Find(p => p.IsMainProviderPackage);
+
+            return content.Replace("[ProviderName]", mainPackage?.UseMethodName ?? string.Empty)
+                .Replace("[ConnectionString]", redactedConnectionString.Replace(@"\", @"\\"))
+                .Replace("[UseList]", useText)
+                .Replace("[PackageList]", packageText.ToString())
+                .Replace("[ContextName]", options.ContextClassName);
+        }
+
+        private static Dictionary<string, string> GetKnownProviders()
+        {
+            var result = new Dictionary<string, string>();
+
+            foreach (var provider in GetProvidersWithAliases())
+            {
+                result.Add(provider.Key, provider.Key);
+
+                foreach (var item in provider.Value)
+                {
+                    result.Add(item, provider.Key);
+                }
+            }
+
+            return result;
+        }
+
+        private static Dictionary<string, List<string>> GetProvidersWithAliases()
+        {
+            return new Dictionary<string, List<string>>
+            {
+                {
+                    "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer",
+                    new List<string> { "mssql", "sqlserver" }
+                },
+                {
+                    "Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Sqlite",
+                    new List<string> { "sqlite" }
+                },
+                {
+                    "Npgsql.EntityFrameworkCore.PostgreSQL",
+                    new List<string> { "postgres", "postgresql" }
+                },
+                {
+                    "Pomelo.EntityFrameworkCore.MySql",
+                    new List<string> { "mysql" }
+                },
+                {
+                    "Oracle.EntityFrameworkCore",
+                    new List<string> { "oracle" }
+                },
+                {
+                    "FirebirdSql.EntityFrameworkCore.Firebird",
+                    new List<string> { "firebird" }
+                },
+                {
+                    "EFCore.Snowflake",
+                    new List<string> { "snowflake" }
+                },
+            };
+        }
